                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>বয়েলের সূত্র অনুসারে <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-9-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>V</mi><mtext>&amp;#xA0;</mtext><mo>&amp;#x221D;</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>P</mi></mfrac></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-145" style="width: 3.199em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.625em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.027em, 1002.62em, 2.502em, -999.998em); top: -2.006em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-146"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-147" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">V</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-148" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">&nbsp;</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-149" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">∝</span><span class="mfrac" id="MathJax-Span-150" style="padding-left: 0.289em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.617em; height: 0px; margin-right: 0.125em; margin-left: 0.125em;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1000.29em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.424em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.162em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-151" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">1</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.404em, 1000.45em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -3.645em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.244em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-152" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">P</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.904em, 1000.62em, 1.191em, -999.998em); top: -1.268em; left: 0em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: 0em; border-top: 1.5px solid; width: 0.617em; height: 0px;"></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.068em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.01em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.497em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.602em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mo>∝</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">P</mi></mfrac></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-9">\rm V\ \propto\frac{1}{P}</script></span><br>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: SATP তে গ্যাসের মোলার আয়তনকে <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-48-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><msubsup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>V</mi><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>m</mi><mtext>&amp;#xA0;</mtext></mrow><mi>&amp;#x03B8;</mi></msubsup></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-644" style="width: 1.6em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.314em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.986em, 1001.31em, 2.256em, -999.998em); top: -1.965em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-645"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-646"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.6em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.199em, 1000.74em, 4.182em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-647" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">V</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.404em, 1000.41em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.383em; left: 0.74em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-648" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">θ</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.568em, 1000.86em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -3.85em; left: 0.74em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-649"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-650"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-651" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">m</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-652" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">&nbsp;</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; [হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-১০]</p>

                                        <br>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: ক্ষারকের শক্তিমাত্রা: <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-58-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>O</mi><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>H</mi><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo></msup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>C</mi><msubsup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>O</mi><mn>3</mn><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mn>2</mn><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>C</mi><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>N</mi><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo></msup><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>N</mi><msub><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>H</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-750" style="width: 12.83em;                                         <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: সরল দোলকের গতি, কঠিন পদার্থের কেলাসের মধ্যে অণু, ডোরাকাটা শার্টের ডোরাগুলোর অবস্থান, ধান ক্ষেতে সৃষ্ট ঢেউয়ের গতি, ইলেকট্রিক পোল ইত্যাদি স্থানিক পর্যায়ক্রমের উদাহরণ।<br>
[তপন স্যার: সংস্করণ- ২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৫৬৩]</p>

</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>কোনো একক নেই</p>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: একই জাতীয় দুটি রাশির অনুপাত হওয়ায় বিকৃতির কোনো একক ও মাত্রা সমীকরণ নেই।<br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ- ২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৪৯১]</p>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>WH question যুক্ত&nbsp;Past Indefinite tense এর&nbsp;passive: By whom + was/were + object হবে subject + v<sub>3</sub></p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Mediocre- মাঝারি; Average - গড়, গড়ের মাধ্যমে আমরা মাঝামাঝি result পাই; Industrious - পরিশ্রমী; Ordinary - সাধারণ; Better - অধিকতর ভালো।</p>

                                    <div class="row">

                                            <span>Question 85 </span>

                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>Even as harvesting was going on _____.</p>

                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>the rainy season began</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>the rainy season was began</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>the rainy season had began</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>the rainy season begins</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Option (b) passive বলে begun হওয়া উচিত। Option (c) তে had + v<sub>3</sub>&nbsp;হবে। Complex sentence এর উভয় clause একই&nbsp;verb গ্রহণ করে। তাই সঠিক উত্তর&nbsp;the rainy season began।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>

                                            <p>"Do not close the door". The correct passive form of the sentence is-</p>

                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Let not the door be closed.</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">

                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Let the door not to be closed.</p>

                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Le not the door closed.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Let not the door to be closing.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Imperative sentence do not/don't দিয়ে শুরু হলে তার Passive করার ক্ষেত্রে Let not দিয়ে শুরু করতে হয়।<br>
Let not + obj+ be + v<sub>3</sub></p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>

                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>বাংলাদেশ ১৯৭২ সালের ১৮ এপ্রিল প্রথম আন্তর্জাতিক সংস্থা হিসেবে কমনওয়েলথের ৩২ তম সদস্যপদ লাভ করে।</p>
